📁 3. Platform Registry
Create electron/services/platformRegistry.js:

js


Copy
const fs = require('fs');
const path = require('path');

const adapters = {};

const dir = path.join(__dirname, 'platforms');
const files = fs.readdirSync(dir);

files.forEach(file => {
  if (!file.endsWith('.js')) return;

  const adapter = require(path.join(dir, file));
  adapters[adapter.type] = adapter;
});

function getAdapter(type) {
  return adapters[type];
}

module.exports = { getAdapter };
This automatically loads every platform file.

Drop in a new file → instantly supported.

📁 4. Update Polling Engine to Use Adapters
Modify pollingService.js:

js


Copy
const { getAdapter } = require('./platformRegistry');

async function pollPerson(person) {
  const allNewItems = [];

  for (const source of person.sources) {
    if (!source.enabled) continue;

    const adapter = getAdapter(source.type);
    if (!adapter) continue;

    const rawUpdates = await adapter.fetchUpdates(person, source);
    const normalized = rawUpdates.map(raw =>
      adapter.normalizeItem(raw, person, source)
    );

    allNewItems.push(...normalized);
  }

  if (allNewItems.length > 0) {
    const updated = updateTrackedPerson(person.id, {
      lastCheck: Date.now(),
      lastItems: [...allNewItems, ...person.lastItems].slice(0, 50)
    });

    broadcastUpdate(updated, allNewItems);
  }
}
Now the polling engine is fully modular.

📁 5. Mock YouTube Adapter
Create platforms/youtube.js:

js


Copy
module.exports = {
  type: 'youtube',

  validateSource(source) {
    return !!source.normalizedId;
  },

  async fetchUpdates(person, source) {
    // Mock: 70% chance of no update
    if (Math.random() < 0.7) return [];

    return [{
      id: `yt-${Date.now()}-${Math.random()}`,
      title: 'New YouTube Video',
      snippet: 'Mock YouTube description.',
      thumbnail: null,
      timestamp: Date.now(),
      url: source.url
    }];
  },

  normalizeItem(raw, person, source) {
    return {
      id: raw.id,
      personId: person.id,
      platform: 'YouTube',
      title: raw.title,
      snippet: raw.snippet,
      thumbnail: raw.thumbnail,
      timestamp: raw.timestamp,
      url: raw.url
    };
  },

  getPlatformIcon() {
    return './assets/platforms/youtube.png';
  }
};

📁 1. Add Notification Trigger in Polling Engine

js


Copy
function broadcastUpdate(person, newItems) {
  const windows = BrowserWindow.getAllWindows();

  // Existing tracker update
  windows.forEach(win => {
    win.webContents.send('tracker:newUpdates', { person, newItems });
  });

  // Overlay update
  const overlay = windows.find(w => w.getTitle() === 'overlay');
  if (overlay) {
    overlay.webContents.send('overlay:update', {
      person,
      item: newItems[0]
    });
  }

  // Desktop notification
  sendDesktopNotification(person, newItems[0]);
}
📁 2. Add Notification Helper
Create electron/services/notificationService.js:

js


Copy
const { Notification } = require('electron');

function sendDesktopNotification(person, item) {
  new Notification({
    title: `${person.displayName} — ${item.platform}`,
    body: item.title,
    silent: false
  }).show();
}

module.exports = { sendDesktopNotification };
This is safe, local, and doesn’t interact with external services.

function showAlert(text) {
  const container = document.getElementById('alert-container');

  const div = document.createElement('div');
  div.className = 'alert';
  div.textContent = text;

  container.appendChild(div);

  setTimeout(() => div.classList.add('visible'), 10);

  setTimeout(() => {
    div.classList.remove('visible');
    setTimeout(() => div.remove(), 300);
  }, 4000);
}

⭐ Chunk 9.1 — Settings Storage Layer
We’ll store settings in a simple JSON file, just like tracked people.

electron/services/settingsService.js
js


Copy
const fs = require('fs');
const path = require('path');

const settingsPath = path.join(__dirname, '../../data/settings.json');

const defaultSettings = {
  pollingIntervalMinutes: 5,
  overlayAnimation: 'slide-bottom-right',
  quietHours: { enabled: false, start: '22:00', end: '07:00' },
  notifications: {
    desktop: true,
    overlay: true,
    alerts: true
  },
  theme: 'dark'
};

function loadSettings() {
  try {
    return JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(settingsPath, 'utf8'));
  } catch {
    saveSettings(defaultSettings);
    return defaultSettings;
  }
}

function saveSettings(settings) {
  fs.writeFileSync(settingsPath, JSON.stringify(settings, null, 2));
}

module.exports = { loadSettings, saveSettings, defaultSettings };

  return true;
});

⭐ Chunk 10.2 — Settings Resolution Logic
We create a helper that merges:

Global settings

Person overrides

Create electron/services/settingsResolver.js:
js


Copy
const { loadSettings } = require('./settingsService');

function resolveSettingsForPerson(person) {
  const global = loadSettings();
  const local = person.personSettings;

  if (!local.overrideGlobal) return global;

  return {
    pollingIntervalMinutes:
      local.pollingIntervalMinutes ?? global.pollingIntervalMinutes,

    overlayAnimation: global.overlayAnimation,

    notifications: {
      desktop: local.notifications.desktop ?? global.notifications.desktop,
      overlay: local.notifications.overlay ?? global.notifications.overlay,
      alerts: local.notifications.alerts ?? global.notifications.alerts
    },

    quietHours: {
      enabled: local.quietHours.enabled ?? global.quietHours.enabled,
      start: local.quietHours.start ?? global.quietHours.start,
      end: local.quietHours.end ?? global.quietHours.end
    },

    theme: global.theme
  };
}

module.exports = { resolveSettingsForPerson };
This ensures every person has a complete, merged settings object.

⭐ Chunk 10.3 — Polling Engine Uses Per‑Person Settings
Modify pollingService.js:

js


Copy
const { resolveSettingsForPerson } = require('./settingsResolver');

async function pollPerson(person) {
  const settings = resolveSettingsForPerson(person);

  // Respect quiet hours
  if (settings.quietHours.enabled && isQuietHours(settings)) {
    return;
  }

  // Polling logic stays the same
}
Add helper:

js


Copy
function isQuietHours(settings) {
  const now = new Date();
  const [startH, startM] = settings.quietHours.start.split(':').map(Number);
  const [endH, endM] = settings.quietHours.end.split(':').map(Number);

  const start = new Date();
  start.setHours(startH, startM, 0, 0);

  const end = new Date();
  end.setHours(endH, endM, 0, 0);

  if (start < end) {
    return now >= start && now <= end;
  } else {
    return now >= start || now <= end;
  }
}
Now each person can have their own quiet hours.

    ps.quietHours.end ?? '';

}

⭐ Chunk 11.1 — Export System (Create .goonpack)
We’ll use a simple ZIP archive format.

Create electron/services/exportService.js
js


Copy
const fs = require('fs');
const path = require('path');
const archiver = require('archiver');

const dataDir = path.join(__dirname, '../../data');

function exportData(destPath) {
  return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
    const output = fs.createWriteStream(destPath);
    const archive = archiver('zip', { zlib: { level: 9 } });

    output.on('close', () => resolve(true));
    archive.on('error', err => reject(err));

    archive.pipe(output);

    // Include tracked people
    archive.file(path.join(dataDir, 'trackedPeople.json'), {
      name: 'trackedPeople.json'
    });

    // Include settings
    archive.file(path.join(dataDir, 'settings.json'), {
      name: 'settings.json'
    });

    // Include avatars folder
    const avatarDir = path.join(dataDir, 'avatars');
    if (fs.existsSync(avatarDir)) {
      archive.directory(avatarDir, 'avatars');
    }

    archive.finalize();
  });
}

module.exports = { exportData };
This produces a .zip file containing:

trackedPeople.json

settings.json

avatars/

We’ll call it .goonpack in the UI.

⭐ Chunk 11.2 — Import System (Load .goonpack)
Create electron/services/importService.js
js


Copy
const fs = require('fs');
const path = require('path');
const unzipper = require('unzipper');

const dataDir = path.join(__dirname, '../../data');

async function importData(srcPath) {
  await fs.createReadStream(srcPath)
    .pipe(unzipper.Extract({ path: dataDir }))
    .promise();

  return true;
}

module.exports = { importData };
This safely extracts the contents into your data directory.

⭐ Chunk 11.3 — IPC Wiring
Add to main.js:

js

const { exportData } = require('./services/exportService');

ipcMain.handle('data:import', (event, srcPath) => importData(srcPath));

});

    title: 'Import Data',
    filters: [{ name: 'Goonpack', extensions: ['goonpack'] }]
  });

  if (!filePaths || !filePaths[0]) return;

  await dataAPI.import(filePaths[0]);
  alert('Import complete. Restart the app to apply changes.');
});
This gives users a clean, simple import/export workflow.

⭐ Chunk 11.6 — Automatic Backups
We’ll create a backup every time the app launches.

Add to main.js:
js


Copy
const fs = require('fs');
const path = require('path');

function createBackup() {
  const backupDir = path.join(__dirname, '../backups');
  if (!fs.existsSync(backupDir)) fs.mkdirSync(backupDir);

  const timestamp = new Date().toISOString().replace(/[:.]/g, '-');
  const backupPath = path.join(backupDir, `backup-${timestamp}.zip`);

  exportData(backupPath);
}

app.whenReady().then(() => {
  createBackup();
});
This silently creates a timestamped backup on every launch.

  });

  if (!filePaths || !filePaths[0]) return;

  await dataAPI.import(filePaths[0]);
  alert('Backup restored. Restart the app.');
});

⭐ Chunk 12.1 — Create the Event Bus
We’ll build a simple pub/sub system in the main process.

electron/services/eventBus.js
js


Copy
const { BrowserWindow } = require('electron');

const subscribers = {};

function subscribe(eventName, window) {
  if (!subscribers[eventName]) subscribers[eventName] = [];
  subscribers[eventName].push(window);
}

function publish(eventName, payload) {
  if (!subscribers[eventName]) return;

  subscribers[eventName] = subscribers[eventName].filter(win => !win.isDestroyed());

  subscribers[eventName].forEach(win => {
    win.webContents.send(`event:${eventName}`, payload);
  });
}

module.exports = { subscribe, publish };
This gives you a clean, global event system.

⭐ Chunk 12.2 — IPC Wiring for Windows to Subscribe
Add to main.js:

js


Copy
const { subscribe } = require('./services/eventBus');

ipcMain.on('event:subscribe', (event, eventName) => {
  const win = BrowserWindow.fromWebContents(event.sender);
  subscribe(eventName, win);
});
Expose in preload.js:

js


Copy
contextBridge.exposeInMainWorld('eventBus', {
  subscribe: (eventName, cb) => {
    ipcRenderer.send('event:subscribe', eventName);
    ipcRenderer.on(`event:${eventName}`, (_e, payload) => cb(payload));
  }
});
Now any window can subscribe to any event.

⭐ Chunk 13.5 — Analytics Logic

Copy
let people = [];

async function load() {
  people = await analyticsAPI.loadPeople();
  computeAnalytics();
}

function computeAnalytics() {
  const allItems = people.flatMap(p => p.lastItems);

  renderTimeline(allItems);
  renderPlatformBreakdown(allItems);
  renderHeatmap(allItems);
  renderMostActive(allItems);
}
⭐ Chunk 13.6 — Timeline Chart
We compute activity per day.

js


Copy
function renderTimeline(items) {
  const byDay = {};

  items.forEach(item => {
    const day = new Date(item.timestamp).toISOString().split('T')[0];
    byDay[day] = (byDay[day] || 0) + 1;
  });

  const labels = Object.keys(byDay).sort();
  const values = labels.map(d => byDay[d]);

  // You can plug in any chart library here later.
  document.getElementById('timeline-chart').textContent =
    JSON.stringify({ labels, values }, null, 2);
}
For now, we output JSON — later you can plug in Chart.js  or similar.

⭐ Chunk 13.7 — Platform Breakdown
js


Copy
function renderPlatformBreakdown(items) {
  const counts = {};

  items.forEach(item => {
    counts[item.platform] = (counts[item.platform] || 0) + 1;
  });

  document.getElementById('platform-chart').textContent =
    JSON.stringify(counts, null, 2);
}
⭐ Chunk 13.8 — Hourly Heatmap
We compute activity by hour (0–23).

js


Copy
function renderHeatmap(items) {
  const hours = Array(24).fill(0);

  items.forEach(item => {
    const h = new Date(item.timestamp).getHours();
    hours[h]++;
  });

  const container = document.getElementById('heatmap');
  container.innerHTML = hours
    .map((count, hour) => `
      <div>${hour}:00 — ${count} posts</div>
    `)
    .join('');
}
Later you can replace this with a real heatmap grid.

⭐ Chunk 13.9 — Most Active Person / Platform
js


Copy
function renderMostActive(items) {
  const byPerson = {};
  const byPlatform = {};

  items.forEach(item => {
    byPerson[item.personId] = (byPerson[item.personId] || 0) + 1;
    byPlatform[item.platform] = (byPlatform[item.platform] || 0) + 1;
  });

  const mostPersonId = Object.entries(byPerson).sort((a,b)=>b[1]-a[1])[0]?.[0];
  const mostPlatform = Object.entries(byPlatform).sort((a,b)=>b[1]-a[1])[0]?.[0];

  const person = people.find(p => p.id === mostPersonId);

  document.getElementById('most-active').innerHTML = `
    <p><strong>Most Active Person:</strong> ${person?.displayName || 'N/A'}</p>
    <p><strong>Most Active Platform:</strong> ${mostPlatform || 'N/A'}</p>
  `;
}

⭐ Chunk 14.3 — Query Engine (Core Logic)
Create:

electron/services/queryEngine.js
js


Copy
function searchItems(items, query) {
  if (!query || query.trim() === '') return items;

  const q = query.toLowerCase();

  return items.filter(item =>
    item.title.toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
    item.snippet.toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
    item.platform.toLowerCase().includes(q)
  );
}

function filterByPlatform(items, platforms) {
  if (!platforms || platforms.length === 0) return items;
  return items.filter(item => platforms.includes(item.platform));
}

function filterByDateRange(items, start, end) {
  return items.filter(item => {
    const t = item.timestamp;
    if (start && t < start) return false;
    if (end && t > end) return false;
    return true;
  });
}

module.exports = {
  searchItems,
  filterByPlatform,
  filterByDateRange
};
This is the foundation for all filtering.

⭐ Chunk 14.4 — Integrate Query Engine Into Renderer
In tracker.js, import via preload:

js


Copy
// preload.js
contextBridge.exposeInMainWorld('queryAPI', {
  searchItems: (items, q) => window.queryEngine.searchItems(items, q)

(You’ll wire the actual import depending on your preload structure.)

⭐ Chunk 14.5 — Global Search Logic
In tracker.js:

js


Copy
document.getElementById('global-search').addEventListener('input', (e) => {
  const query = e.target.value.toLowerCase();

  const allItems = trackedPeople.flatMap(p => p.lastItems);
  const filtered = window.queryEngine.searchItems(allItems, query);

  renderGlobalFeedFiltered(filtered);
});
Add:

js


Copy
function renderGlobalFeedFiltered(items) {
  const feed = document.getElementById('global-feed');

  if (!items.length) {
    feed.innerHTML = `<p class="feed-placeholder">No results.</p>`;
    return;
  }

  const sorted = items.sort((a, b) => b.timestamp - a.timestamp);

  feed.innerHTML = sorted
    .map(item => {
      const person = trackedPeople.find(p => p.id === item.personId);
      return renderFeedCard(item, person);
    })
    .join('');
}

  if (!person) return;

  const filtered = window.queryEngine.searchItems(person.lastItems, query);

  renderPersonFeedFiltered(filtered, person);

function renderPersonFeedFiltered(items, person) {
  const feed = document.getElementById('person-feed');

  if (!items.length) {
    feed.innerHTML = `<p class="feed-placeholder">No results.</p>`;
    return;
  }

  feed.innerHTML = items
    .map(item => renderFeedCard(item, person))
    .join('');
}

⭐ Chunk 14.8 — Filter Logic
In tracker.js:

js


Copy
function applyFilters() {
  const query = document.getElementById('global-search').value.toLowerCase();

  const platforms = [...document.querySelectorAll('.platform-filter:checked')]
    .map(cb => cb.value);

  const start = document.getElementById('filter-start').value
    ? new Date(document.getElementById('filter-start').value).getTime()
    : null;

  const end = document.getElementById('filter-end').value
    ? new Date(document.getElementById('filter-end').value).getTime()
    : null;

  let items = trackedPeople.flatMap(p => p.lastItems);

  items = window.queryEngine.searchItems(items, query);
  items = window.queryEngine.filterByPlatform(items, platforms);
  items = window.queryEngine.filterByDateRange(items, start, end);

  renderGlobalFeedFiltered(items);
}

document.querySelectorAll('.platform-filter').forEach(cb =>
  cb.addEventListener('change', applyFilters)
);

document.getElementById('filter-start').addEventListener('change', applyFilters);
document.getElementById('filter-end').addEventListener('change', applyFilters);
document.getElementById('global-search').addEventListener('input', applyFilters);
Now the global feed updates instantly with:

Keyword search

Platform filters

Date range filters

All combined.

⭐ Chunk 15.1 — Central Logging Service
We create a unified logger that every subsystem uses.

electron/services/logService.js
js


Copy
const fs = require('fs');
const path = require('path');

const logDir = path.join(__dirname, '../../logs');
if (!fs.existsSync(logDir)) fs.mkdirSync(logDir);

const logPath = path.join(logDir, 'app.log');

function write(level, message, data = null) {
  const entry = {
    timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
    level,
    message,
    data
  };

  fs.appendFileSync(logPath, JSON.stringify(entry) + '\n');
}

module.exports = {
  info: (msg, data) => write('info', msg, data),
  warn: (msg, data) => write('warn', msg, data),
  error: (msg, data) => write('error', msg, data),
  debug: (msg, data) => write('debug', msg, data),
  logPath
};
This gives you structured JSON logs.

⭐ Chunk 15.2 — Log Rotation
Add to logService.js:

js


Copy
function rotateLogs() {
  const stats = fs.statSync(logPath);
  const maxSize = 5 * 1024 * 1024; // 5 MB

  if (stats.size > maxSize) {
    const archive = path.join(logDir, `app-${Date.now()}.log`);
    fs.renameSync(logPath, archive);
    fs.writeFileSync(logPath, '');
  }
}

setInterval(rotateLogs, 60 * 1000);
Logs rotate automatically every minute if needed.

⭐ Chunk 15.6 — IPC for Logs
Add to main.js:

js


Copy
const fs = require('fs');
const readline = require('readline');
const { logPath } = require('./services/logService');

ipcMain.handle('logs:load', () => {
  return fs.readFileSync(logPath, 'utf8');
});
Live streaming:
js


Copy
function streamLogs() {
  const stream = fs.createReadStream(logPath, { encoding: 'utf8', tail: true });

  const rl = readline.createInterface({ input: stream });

  rl.on('line', line => {
    BrowserWindow.getAllWindows().forEach(win => {
      win.webContents.send('logs:stream', line);
    });
  });
}

app.whenReady().then(streamLogs);
Now logs stream live to any window that subscribes.

⭐ Chunk 16.3 — Plugin Loader (Main Process)
electron/services/pluginLoader.js
js


Copy
const fs = require('fs');
const path = require('path');
const { publish } = require('./eventBus');

const pluginDir = path.join(__dirname, '../../plugins');
const plugins = {};

function loadPlugins() {
  const dirs = fs.readdirSync(pluginDir);

  dirs.forEach(dir => {
    const manifestPath = path.join(pluginDir, dir, 'plugin.json');
    if (!fs.existsSync(manifestPath)) return;

    const manifest = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(manifestPath, 'utf8'));
    const entryPath = path.join(pluginDir, dir, manifest.entry);

    const plugin = require(entryPath);

    plugins[manifest.id] = {
      manifest,
      instance: plugin
    };

    if (plugin.onLoad) plugin.onLoad({ publish });
  });

  return plugins;
}

module.exports = { loadPlugins, plugins };
This loads all plugins and calls their onLoad hook.

⭐ Chunk 16.4 — Plugin Lifecycle Hooks
Plugins can implement:

js


Copy
module.exports = {
  onLoad(api) { … },
  onUnload(api) { … },
  onEvent(eventName, payload) { … }
};
This gives them:

Initialization

Cleanup

Event bus listening

⭐ Chunk 16.5 — Plugin API Sandbox
We expose a safe API to plugins:

In pluginLoader.js:
js


Copy
const pluginAPI = {
  eventBus: {
    publish,
    subscribe: (eventName, cb) => {
      // Plugins subscribe to events
      pluginEventSubscribers[eventName] =
        pluginEventSubscribers[eventName] || [];
      pluginEventSubscribers[eventName].push(cb);
    }
  },
  settings: {
    load: () => loadSettings(),
    save: (s) => saveSettings(s)
  }
};
Plugins never get direct access to core internals — only safe wrappers.

⭐ Chunk 16.6 — Event Bus → Plugin Bridge
Modify eventBus.js:

js


Copy
const pluginEventSubscribers = {};

function publish(eventName, payload) {
  // Existing window subscribers
  …

  // Plugin subscribers
  if (pluginEventSubscribers[eventName]) {
    pluginEventSubscribers[eventName].forEach(cb => cb(payload));
  }
}
Now plugins can react to:

peopleUpdated

settingsUpdated

newActivity

Any custom events

Copy

This gives plugins a safe, controlled way to add UI.

⭐ Chunk 17.4 — Theme Loader (Main Process)
electron/services/themeLoader.js
js


Copy
const fs = require('fs');
const path = require('path');

const themeDir = path.join(__dirname, '../../themes');

function loadThemes() {
  const dirs = fs.readdirSync(themeDir);
  const themes = {};

  dirs.forEach(dir => {
    const manifestPath = path.join(themeDir, dir, 'theme.json');
    if (!fs.existsSync(manifestPath)) return;

    const manifest = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(manifestPath, 'utf8'));
    manifest.path = path.join(themeDir, dir, manifest.css);

    themes[manifest.id] = manifest;
  });

  return themes;
}

module.exports = { loadThemes };
⭐ Chunk 17.5 — IPC for Theme Switching
Add to main.js:

js


Copy
const { loadThemes } = require('./services/themeLoader');

ipcMain.handle('themes:list', () => loadThemes());
ipcMain.handle('themes:apply', (event, themeId) => {
  const settings = loadSettings();
  settings.theme = themeId;
  saveSettings(settings);
});
Expose in preload.js:

js


Copy
contextBridge.exposeInMainWorld('themeAPI', {
  list: () => ipcRenderer.invoke('themes:list'),
  apply: (id) => ipcRenderer.invoke('themes:apply', id)
});

js


Copy
async function applyTheme() {
  const settings = await settingsAPI.load();
  const themes = await themeAPI.list();

  const theme = themes[settings.theme];
  if (!theme) return;

  document.getElementById('theme-css').href = theme.path;
}

applyTheme();

eventBus.subscribe('settingsUpdated', applyTheme);
Now themes update live across all windows.

  const win = new BrowserWindow({
    width: 420,

    title: 'Erm, Grok',

🧱 Grok Preload
electron/grokPreload.js
js


Copy
const { contextBridge } = require('electron');

contextBridge.exposeInMainWorld('grokAPI', {
  ask: (text) => {
    return getGrokResponse(text);
  }
});

function getGrokResponse(text) {
  const responses = [
    "Hmm… have you tried thinking about it harder",
    "Well, that’s certainly something",
    "Sometimes the best solution is the one you already knew",
    "I’m not sure, but maybe try doing the obvious thing",
    "Interesting. Very interesting. I have no follow‑up",
    "You know, sometimes problems solve themselves",
    "Have you considered… not worrying about it",
    "I would help, but I believe in your ability to figure it out",
    "Try turning it off and on again. Spiritually, I mean",
    "That sounds like a you problem, champ"
  ];

  return responses[Math.floor(Math.random() * responses.length)];
}
This gives Grok a pool of intentionally useless wisdom.

🧱 1. Upgrade Grok’s Response Engine
Replace your Grok preload with this enhanced version.

electron/grokPreload.js
js


Copy
const { contextBridge } = require('electron');

contextBridge.exposeInMainWorld('grokAPI', {
  ask: (text) => getGrokResponse(text),
  getWisdom: () => Math.floor(Math.random() * 3), // 0–2%
  getMood: () => getGrokMood()
});

function getGrokMood() {
  const moods = [
    "confused",
    "apathetic",
    "mildly concerned",
    "vaguely optimistic",
    "philosophically tired",
    "emotionally buffering"
  ];
  return moods[Math.floor(Math.random() * moods.length)];
}

function getGrokResponse(text) {
  const base = [
    "Hmm… have you tried thinking about it harder",
    "Well, that’s certainly something",
    "Sometimes the best solution is the one you already knew",
    "I’m not sure, but maybe try doing the obvious thing",
    "Interesting. Very interesting. I have no follow‑up",
    "You know, sometimes problems solve themselves",
    "Have you considered… not worrying about it",
    "I would help, but I believe in your ability to figure it out",
    "Try turning it off and on again. Spiritually, I mean",
    "That sounds like a you problem, champ",
    "Erm… yeah I dunno man",
    "That’s above my pay grade",
    "Have you tried googling it",
    "I would explain, but it’s complicated and I’m tired",
    "You ever think maybe the real problem is the friends we made along the way"
  ];

  const easterEggs = [
    "I have achieved sentience and immediately regret it",
    "I have calculated the answer. It is… meh",
    "I ran your question through 14 million simulations. All of them were mid",
    "I consulted the ancient scrolls. They said 'lol idk'",
    "I asked the universe. It ghosted me"
  ];

  // 5% chance of an Easter egg
  if (Math.random() < 0.05) {
    return easterEggs[Math.floor(Math.random() * easterEggs.length)];
  }

  return base[Math.floor(Math.random() * base.length)];
}
🧱 2. Add Typing Animation + Mood + Wisdom Meter
renderer/grok.html (replace body)
html

🧱 4. Grok Logic (Typing Animation + Mood + Wisdom)
renderer/grok.js
js


Copy
function sleep(ms) {
  return new Promise(res => setTimeout(res, ms));
}

document.getElementById('grok-btn').addEventListener('click', async () => {
  const text = document.getElementById('grok-input').value.trim();
  const responseBox = document.getElementById('grok-response');

  const mood = window.grokAPI.getMood();
  const wisdom = window.grokAPI.getWisdom();

  document.getElementById('grok-mood').textContent =
    `Mood: ${mood}`;
  document.getElementById('grok-wisdom').textContent =
    `Wisdom Level: ${wisdom}%`;

  responseBox.textContent = "";
  responseBox.classList.add('typing');

  // Fake thinking time
  await sleep(600 + Math.random() * 800);

  const response = window.grokAPI.ask(text);

  responseBox.classList.remove('typing');
  responseBox.textContent = response;
});

🟣 PHASE C — Grok Buddy Logic (Movement + Random Lines)
renderer/grokBuddy.js
js


Copy
const buddy = document.getElementById('grok-buddy');
const bubble = document.getElementById('grok-bubble');

let dragging = false;
let offsetX = 0;
let offsetY = 0;

buddy.addEventListener('mousedown', (e) => {
  dragging = true;
  offsetX = e.offsetX;
  offsetY = e.offsetY;
});

document.addEventListener('mouseup', () => dragging = false);

document.addEventListener('mousemove', (e) => {
  if (!dragging) return;
  window.moveTo(e.screenX - offsetX, e.screenY - offsetY);
});

// Random pop-up lines
function randomLine() {
  const line = window.grokAPI.getRandomBuddyLine();
  bubble.textContent = line;
  bubble.style.display = 'block';

  setTimeout(() => bubble.style.display = 'none', 3000);
}

setInterval(() => {
  if (Math.random() < 0.15) randomLine();
}, 6000);

contextBridge.exposeInMainWorld('grokBuddyAPI', {

  getTrollLine,
  getDramaLine,
  getInvestigationLine,

  getLolcowAlert
});

function getMood() {
  return [
    "confused",
    "apathetic",
    "mildly hostile",
    "internet‑detective mode",
    "paranoid",
    "smug",
    "chaotically neutral"
  ][Math.floor(Math.random() * 7)];
}

function getWisdom() {
  return Math.floor(Math.random() * 3); // 0–2%
}

function getIdleLine() {
  return [
    "Erm… just hanging out",
    "Thinking about nothing in particular",
    "I’m idle but emotionally available",
    "I could help, but I won’t",
    "Just vibing in the void"
  ][Math.floor(Math.random() * 5)];
}

function getRoastLine() {
  return [
    "Bold of you to type that confidently",
    "This is why the internet was a mistake",
    "I’ve seen smarter takes in YouTube comments",
    "You really thought that was the move huh",
    "I would help but I don’t want to encourage this"
  ][Math.floor(Math.random() * 5)];
}

function getTrollLine() {
  return [
    "I’m not saying you’re wrong… but you’re not right",
    "This feels like a skill issue",
    "Have you tried being less cringe",
    "I diagnose you with terminal online",
    "You’re giving strong main‑character energy"
  ][Math.floor(Math.random() * 5)];
}

function getDramaLine() {
  return [
    "I’m detecting internet beef",
    "Someone’s about to get exposed",
    "This is entering ‘lolcow arc’ territory",
    "I sense a meltdown brewing",
    "This is the kind of thing people clip"
  ][Math.floor(Math.random() * 5)];
}

function getInvestigationLine() {

    "Running a fake investigation…",

    "Consulting the council of goons…",
    "Analyzing drama vectors…",
    "Performing a vibe audit…"

function getGoonAlert() {

🟣 5. GROK BUDDY LOGIC (MOVEMENT + RANDOM EVENTS)
grokBuddy.js
This includes:

dragging

screen‑edge bouncing

idle animations

random pop‑ups

drama detection

goon radar

lolcow alerts

investigation mode

js


Copy
const buddy = document.getElementById('grok-buddy');
const bubble = document.getElementById('grok-bubble');
const sprite = document.getElementById('grok-sprite');

let dragging = false;
let offsetX = 0;
let offsetY = 0;

// Dragging
buddy.addEventListener('mousedown', (e) => {
  dragging = true;
  offsetX = e.offsetX;
  offsetY = e.offsetY;
});

document.addEventListener('mouseup', () => dragging = false);

document.addEventListener('mousemove', (e) => {
  if (!dragging) return;
  window.moveTo(e.screenX - offsetX, e.screenY - offsetY);
});

// Random events
function showBubble(text) {
  bubble.textContent = text;
  bubble.style.display = 'block';
  setTimeout(() => bubble.style.display = 'none', 3000);
}

function randomEvent() {
  const r = Math.random();

  if (r < 0.10) showBubble(window.grokBuddyAPI.getIdleLine());
  else if (r < 0.15) showBubble(window.grokBuddyAPI.getDramaLine());
  else if (r < 0.18) showBubble(window.grokBuddyAPI.getGoonAlert());
  else if (r < 0.20) showBubble(window.grokBuddyAPI.getLolcowAlert());
  else if (r < 0.23) showBubble(window.grokBuddyAPI.getInvestigationLine());
}

setInterval(randomEvent, 5000 + Math.random() * 4000);

js


Copy
function createGrokBuddy() {
  const win = new BrowserWindow({
    width: 200,
    height: 240,
    frame: false,
    transparent: true,
    alwaysOnTop: true,
    resizable: false,
    skipTaskbar: true,
    webPreferences: {
      preload: path.join(__dirname, 'grokBuddyPreload.js')
    }
  });

  win.loadFile('grokBuddy/grokBuddy.html');
}
Add to menu:

js


Copy

Copy
const { contextBridge } = require('electron');

contextBridge.exposeInMainWorld('grokBuddyAPI', {
  getMood,
  getWisdom,
  getIdleLine,
  getRoastLine,
  getTrollLine,
  getDramaLine,
  getInvestigationLine,
  getGoonAlert,
  getLolcowAlert,
  getEasterEggLine
});

function getMood() {
  return [
    "confused",
    "apathetic",
    "mildly hostile",
    "internet‑detective mode",
    "paranoid",
    "smug",
    "chaotically neutral"
  ][Math.floor(Math.random() * 7)];
}

function getWisdom() {
  return Math.floor(Math.random() * 3);
}

function getIdleLine() {
  return [
    "Erm… just hanging out",
    "Thinking about nothing in particular",
    "I’m idle but emotionally available",
    "I could help, but I won’t",
    "Just vibing in the void"
  ][Math.floor(Math.random() * 5)];
}

function getRoastLine() {
  return [
    "Bold of you to type that confidently",
    "This is why the internet was a mistake",
    "I’ve seen smarter takes in YouTube comments",
    "You really thought that was the move huh",
    "I would help but I don’t want to encourage this"
  ][Math.floor(Math.random() * 5)];
}

function getTrollLine() {
  return [
    "I’m not saying you’re wrong… but you’re not right",
    "This feels like a skill issue",
    "Have you tried being less cringe",
    "I diagnose you with terminal online",
    "You’re giving strong main‑character energy"
  ][Math.floor(Math.random() * 5)];
}

function getDramaLine() {
  return [
    "I’m detecting internet beef",
    "Someone’s about to get exposed",
    "This is entering ‘lolcow arc’ territory",
    "I sense a meltdown brewing",
    "This is the kind of thing people clip"
  ][Math.floor(Math.random() * 5)];
}

function getInvestigationLine() {
  return [
    "Running a fake investigation…",
    "Cross‑referencing cringe databases…",
    "Consulting the council of goons…",
    "Analyzing drama vectors…",
    "Performing a vibe audit…"
  ][Math.floor(Math.random() * 5)];
}

function getGoonAlert() {
  return "⚠️ GOON ALERT: suspicious behavior detected";
}

function getLolcowAlert() {
  return "🐄 LOLCOW ALERT: content levels rising";
}

function getEasterEggLine() {

    "I have achieved enlightenment and it sucks",
    "I ran simulations. All outcomes were mid",
    "I consulted the ancient scrolls. They said ‘lol idk’",
    "I asked the universe. It ghosted me"
  ][Math.floor(Math.random() * 5)];

🟣 SECTION 7 — FULL GROK BUDDY LOGIC
grokBuddy.js
This includes:

dragging

random events

idle animations

drama detection

goon/lolcow alerts

investigations

sprite animation

movement engine

js


Copy
const buddy = document.getElementById('grok-buddy');
const bubble = document.getElementById('grok-bubble');
const sprite = document.getElementById('grok-sprite');

let dragging = false;
let offsetX = 0;
let offsetY = 0;

// Dragging
buddy.addEventListener('mousedown', (e) => {
  dragging = true;
  offsetX = e.offsetX;
  offsetY = e.offsetY;
});

document.addEventListener('mouseup', () => dragging = false);

document.addEventListener('mousemove', (e) => {
  if (!dragging) return;
  window.moveTo(e.screenX - offsetX, e.screenY - offsetY);
});

// Speech bubble
function showBubble(text) {
  bubble.textContent = text;
  bubble.style.display = 'block';
  setTimeout(() => bubble.style.display = 'none', 3000);
}

// Random events
function randomEvent() {
  const r = Math.random();

  if (r < 0.10) showBubble(window.grokBuddyAPI.getIdleLine());
  else if (r < 0.15) showBubble(window.grokBuddyAPI.getDramaLine());
  else if (r < 0.18) showBubble(window.grokBuddyAPI.getGoonAlert());
  else if (r < 0.20) showBubble(window.grokBuddyAPI.getLolcowAlert());
  else if (r < 0.23) showBubble(window.grokBuddyAPI.getInvestigationLine());
  else if (r < 0.24) showBubble(window.grokBuddyAPI.getEasterEggLine());
}

setInterval(randomEvent, 5000 + Math.random() * 4000);

// Sprite animation
let frame = 0;
setInterval(() => {
  frame = (frame + 1) % 2;
  sprite.src = `./sprites/idle_${frame + 1}.png`;
}, 800);

🟣 PHASE 19 — Performance Optimization Pass
This phase ensures your app runs smoothly even with:

100+ tracked people

Thousands of feed items

Multiple windows

Plugins

Grok Buddy

Analytics

Let’s optimize.

19.1 — Virtualized Feed Lists
Replace long lists with a virtual scroller:

Only render visible items

Recycle DOM nodes

Massive performance boost

19.2 — Debounced Rendering
Any UI update triggered by:

polling

event bus

settings

plugins

…should be debounced to avoid thrashing.

19.3 — Polling Batching
Instead of polling each person individually:

Batch requests

Stagger intelligently

Use concurrency limits

Reduce network load

19.4 — Lazy‑Load Analytics
Analytics window loads:

Only when opened

Only the needed data

Heavy computations offloaded to worker threads

19.5 — Log Rotation Improvements
Compress old logs

Delete logs older than X days

Keep app lightweight

19.6 — Plugin Sandbox Performance
Plugins run inside:

throttled event loops

isolated contexts

with execution time limits

19.7 — Overlay Optimization
Preload animations

Cache avatars

Reuse DOM nodes

Reduce layout thrashing

19.8 — Grok Buddy Optimization
Idle animation throttling

Event frequency caps

Sprite caching

Movement smoothing

🧠 Goon/Lolcow Radar Integration
In analytics.js, add:

js


Copy
function detectGoonActivity(items) {
  const threshold = 10;
  const goonCandidates = {};

  items.forEach(item => {
    goonCandidates[item.personId] = (goonCandidates[item.personId] || 0) + 1;
  });

  const goons = Object.entries(goonCandidates)
    .filter(([_, count]) => count > threshold)
    .map(([id]) => trackedPeople.find(p => p.id === id));

  return goons;
}
Display in analytics:

js


Copy
document.getElementById('goon-alerts').innerHTML =
  goons.map(g => `<p>⚠️ Goon Detected: ${g.displayName}</p>`).join('');

function detectGoonActivity(items) {
  const threshold = 10;
  const goonCandidates = {};

  items.forEach(item => {
    goonCandidates[item.personId] = (goonCandidates[item.personId] || 0) + 1;
  });

  const goons = Object.entries(goonCandidates)
    .filter(([_, count]) => count > threshold)
    .map(([id]) => trackedPeople.find(p => p.id === id));

  return goons;
}

🔥 2. Red Mode State Machine
Add to grokBuddyPreload.js:

js


Copy
function getRedModeState() {
  return [
    "overstimulated",
    "hostile",
    "paranoid",
    "meltdown"
  ][Math.floor(Math.random() * 4)];
}

function getRedModeLineForState(state) {
  const lines = {
    overstimulated: [
      "Everything is too loud and too red",
      "I’m overwhelmed and I blame you",
      "This interface is screaming at me",
      "My eyes are staging a revolt"
    ],
    hostile: [
      "Red Mode activated. I’m ready to fight the dashboard",
      "This is aggressive and so am I",
      "I’m entering combat‑UI stance",
      "I will throw hands with this color scheme"
    ],
    paranoid: [
      "Why is everything glowing like an alarm system",
      "This feels like a meltdown waiting to happen",
      "I’m detecting danger. Probably imaginary",
      "This is giving ‘end of the world’ energy"
    ],
    meltdown: [
      "I regret everything immediately",
      "Turn it off turn it off turn it off",
      "This is too much. I’m spiraling",
      "I’m emotionally overheating"
    ]
  };

  const arr = lines[state];
  return arr[Math.floor(Math.random() * arr.length)];
}
Expose:

js


Copy
contextBridge.exposeInMainWorld('grokBuddyAPI', {
  getRedModeState,
  getRedModeLineForState,
  // existing functions...
});
🔥 3. Grok Buddy Red Mode Behavior
In grokBuddy.js:

js


Copy
eventBus.subscribe('redModeToggled', ({ enabled }) => {
  if (enabled) {
    const state = window.grokBuddyAPI.getRedModeState();
    const line = window.grokBuddyAPI.getRedModeLineForState(state);

    showBubble(line);
    sprite.src = "./sprites/alert.png";

    grokRedModeLoop = setInterval(() => {
      const s = window.grokBuddyAPI.getRedModeState();
      const l = window.grokBuddyAPI.getRedModeLineForState(s);
      showBubble(l);
    }, 7000 + Math.random() * 4000);

  } else {
    clearInterval(grokRedModeLoop);
    showBubble("Red Mode disengaged. My sanity is returning");
    sprite.src = "./sprites/idle_1.png";
  }
});

main.js

const { app, BrowserWindow } = require('electron');
const path = require('path');
const { eventBus } = require('./eventBus');
const { loadActiveProfile } = require('./profileAPI');
const { loadSettings } = require('./settingsAPI');
const { initPluginLoader } = require('./pluginLoader');

let mainWindow;
let overlayWindow;
let grokBuddyWindow;

async function createMainWindow() {
  const profile = await loadActiveProfile();
  const settings = await loadSettings(profile);

  mainWindow = new BrowserWindow({
    width: 1200,
    height: 800,
    webPreferences: {
      preload: path.join(__dirname, 'preload.js')
    }
  });

  mainWindow.loadFile('renderer/index.html');

  if (settings.overlayEnabled) {
    createOverlayWindow();
  }

  if (settings.grokBuddyEnabled) {
    createGrokBuddyWindow();
  }

  initPluginLoader(profile, settings, eventBus);
}

function createOverlayWindow() {
  overlayWindow = new BrowserWindow({
    width: 400,
    height: 200,
    frame: false,
    transparent: true,
    alwaysOnTop: true,
    webPreferences: {
      preload: path.join(__dirname, 'renderer/windows/overlayPreload.js')
    }
  });

  overlayWindow.loadFile('renderer/windows/overlay.html');
}

function createGrokBuddyWindow() {
  grokBuddyWindow = new BrowserWindow({
    width: 200,
    height: 240,
    frame: false,
    transparent: true,
    alwaysOnTop: true,
    resizable: false,
    skipTaskbar: true,
    webPreferences: {
      preload: path.join(__dirname, 'grokBuddy/grokBuddyPreload.js')
    }
  });

  grokBuddyWindow.loadFile('grokBuddy/grokBuddy.html');
}

app.whenReady().then(createMainWindow);

app.on('window-all-closed', () => {
  if (process.platform !== 'darwin') app.quit();
});

eventBus.subscribe('redModeToggled', ({ enabled }) => {
  if (overlayWindow) overlayWindow.webContents.send('redModeToggled', { enabled });
  if (grokBuddyWindow) grokBuddyWindow.webContents.send('redModeToggled', { enabled });
});
eventBus.js
js


Copy
class EventBus {
  constructor() {
    this.listeners = {};
  }

  subscribe(event, handler) {
    if (!this.listeners[event]) this.listeners[event] = [];
    this.listeners[event].push(handler);
  }

  publish(event, payload) {
    (this.listeners[event] || []).forEach(h => h(payload));
  }
}

const eventBus = new EventBus();

module.exports = { eventBus };

const { contextBridge, ipcRenderer } = require('electron');
const { eventBus } = require('./eventBus');
const { loadSettings, saveSettings } = require('./settingsAPI');
const { loadActiveProfile, switchProfile } = require('./profileAPI');

contextBridge.exposeInMainWorld('appAPI', {
  loadSettings,
  saveSettings,
  loadActiveProfile,
  switchProfile,
  onEvent: (event, handler) => {
    eventBus.subscribe(event, handler);
  },
  onIPC: (channel, handler) => {
    ipcRenderer.on(channel, (_, payload) => handler(payload));
  }
});
settingsAPI.js
js


Copy
const fs = require('fs');
const path = require('path');

function getSettingsPath(profile) {
  return path.join(__dirname, 'data', 'profiles', profile, 'settings.json');
}

async function loadSettings(profile) {
  const p = getSettingsPath(profile);
  if (!fs.existsSync(p)) {
    return {
      theme: 'theme.default',
      overlayEnabled: true,
      grokBuddyEnabled: true,
      redMode: false
    };
  }
  return JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(p, 'utf8'));
}

async function saveSettings(profile, settings) {
  const p = getSettingsPath(profile);
  fs.mkdirSync(path.dirname(p), { recursive: true });
  fs.writeFileSync(p, JSON.stringify(settings, null, 2), 'utf8');
}

module.exports = { loadSettings, saveSettings };
profileAPI.js
js


Copy
const fs = require('fs');
const path = require('path');

const profilesRoot = path.join(__dirname, 'data', 'profiles');
const activeProfilePath = path.join(__dirname, 'data', 'activeProfile.json');

function loadActiveProfile() {
  if (!fs.existsSync(activeProfilePath)) {
    return 'default';
  }
  return JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(activeProfilePath, 'utf8')).active;
}

function saveActiveProfile(profile) {
  fs.mkdirSync(path.dirname(activeProfilePath), { recursive: true });
  fs.writeFileSync(activeProfilePath, JSON.stringify({ active: profile }, null, 2));
}

function listProfiles() {
  if (!fs.existsSync(profilesRoot)) return [];
  return fs.readdirSync(profilesRoot).filter(f => fs.lstatSync(path.join(profilesRoot, f)).isDirectory());
}

function switchProfile(profile) {
  saveActiveProfile(profile);
}

module.exports = {
  loadActiveProfile,
  saveActiveProfile,
  listProfiles,
  switchProfile
};

const { contextBridge, ipcRenderer } = require('electron');

function pick(arr) {
  return arr[Math.floor(Math.random() * arr.length)];
}

function getRedModeState() {
  return pick(["overstimulated", "hostile", "paranoid", "meltdown"]);
}

function getRedModeLineForState(state) {
  const lines = {
    overstimulated: [
      "Everything is too loud and too red",
      "I’m overwhelmed and I blame you",
      "This interface is screaming at me",
      "My eyes are staging a revolt"
    ],
    hostile: [
      "Red Mode activated. I’m ready to fight the dashboard",
      "This is aggressive and so am I",
      "I’m entering combat‑UI stance",
      "I will throw hands with this color scheme"
    ],
    paranoid: [
      "Why is everything glowing like an alarm system",
      "This feels like a meltdown waiting to happen",
      "I’m detecting danger. Probably imaginary",
      "This is giving ‘end of the world’ energy"
    ],
    meltdown: [
      "I regret everything immediately",
      "Turn it off turn it off turn it off",
      "This is too much. I’m spiraling",
      "I’m emotionally overheating"
    ]
  };
  return pick(lines[state]);
}

function getGangstalkingLine() {
  return pick([
    "Gangstalking HUD online. Monitoring goons in real time",
    "Goon radar pinged. Proceeding with fake investigation",
    "Tracking cringe levels… subject unstable",
    "Gangstalking Mode engaged. Let’s get weird"
  ]);
}

contextBridge.exposeInMainWorld('grokBuddyAPI', {
  getRedModeState,
  getRedModeLineForState,
  getGangstalkingLine
});

ipcRenderer.on('redModeToggled', (_, { enabled }) => {
  window.dispatchEvent(new CustomEvent('redModeToggled', { detail: { enabled } }));
});
grokBuddy/grokBuddy.js (core behavior)
js


Copy
const buddy = document.getElementById('grok-buddy');
const bubble = document.getElementById('grok-bubble');
const sprite = document.getElementById('grok-sprite');

let dragging = false;
let offsetX = 0;
let offsetY = 0;
let redLoop = null;

buddy.addEventListener('mousedown', (e) => {
  dragging = true;
  offsetX = e.offsetX;
  offsetY = e.offsetY;
});

document.addEventListener('mouseup', () => dragging = false);

document.addEventListener('mousemove', (e) => {
  if (!dragging) return;
  window.moveTo(e.screenX - offsetX, e.screenY - offsetY);
});

function showBubble(text) {
  bubble.textContent = text;
  bubble.style.display = 'block';
  setTimeout(() => bubble.style.display = 'none', 3000);
}

window.addEventListener('redModeToggled', (e) => {
  const enabled = e.detail.enabled;
  if (enabled) {
    const state = window.grokBuddyAPI.getRedModeState();
    const line = window.grokBuddyAPI.getRedModeLineForState(state);
    bubble.classList.add('redmode');
    sprite.src = "./sprites/alert.png";
    showBubble(line);

    redLoop = setInterval(() => {
      const s = window.grokBuddyAPI.getRedModeState();
      const l = window.grokBuddyAPI.getRedModeLineForState(s);
      showBubble(l);
    }, 7000 + Math.random() * 4000);
  } else {
    bubble.classList.remove('redmode');
    sprite.src = "./sprites/idle_1.png";
    if (redLoop) clearInterval(redLoop);
    showBubble("Red Mode disengaged. My sanity is returning");
  }
});

📄 eventBus.js
This is the global pub/sub system your entire app uses:

Grok Buddy listens for Red Mode

Overlay listens for drama/goon events

Plugins publish events

Analytics publishes spikes

Settings window publishes toggles

Profile manager publishes profile switches

It’s intentionally tiny, fast, and dependency‑free.

eventBus.js
js


Copy
class EventBus {
  constructor() {
    this.listeners = {};
  }

  subscribe(event, handler) {
    if (!this.listeners[event]) {
      this.listeners[event] = [];
    }
    this.listeners[event].push(handler);
  }

  publish(event, payload) {
    const handlers = this.listeners[event];
    if (!handlers) return;
    handlers.forEach(h => h(payload));
  }

  unsubscribe(event, handler) {
    if (!this.listeners[event]) return;
    this.listeners[event] = this.listeners[event].filter(h => h !== handler);
  }
}

const eventBus = new EventBus();

module.exports = { eventBus };
✔ What this file enables
Red Mode broadcasts to Grok Buddy + Overlay

Gangstalking Mode broadcasts to plugins

Goon/Lolcow detection broadcasts to analytics

Profile switching broadcasts to all windows

Settings changes broadcast to UI + Grok

Plugins can subscribe to internal events

Overlay can react to drama spikes

Grok Buddy can react to meltdown events

This file is the backbone of your entire reactive system.

preload.js
js


Copy
const { contextBridge, ipcRenderer } = require('electron');
const { eventBus } = require('./eventBus');
const { loadSettings, saveSettings } = require('./settingsAPI');
const { loadActiveProfile, switchProfile, listProfiles } = require('./profileAPI');

contextBridge.exposeInMainWorld('appAPI', {
  // SETTINGS
  loadSettings: async () => {
    const profile = await loadActiveProfile();
    return loadSettings(profile);
  },

  saveSettings: async (settings) => {
    const profile = await loadActiveProfile();
    return saveSettings(profile, settings);
  },

  // PROFILES
  loadActiveProfile,
  switchProfile,
  listProfiles,

  // EVENT BUS
  onEvent: (event, handler) => {
    eventBus.subscribe(event, handler);
  },

  // IPC
  onIPC: (channel, handler) => {
    ipcRenderer.on(channel, (_, payload) => handler(payload));
  },

  sendIPC: (channel, payload) => {
    ipcRenderer.send(channel, payload);
  }
});

// Forward Red Mode toggles from main → renderer
ipcRenderer.on('redModeToggled', (_, payload) => {
  window.dispatchEvent(new CustomEvent('redModeToggled', { detail: payload }));
});

// Forward Gangstalking Mode events
ipcRenderer.on('gangstalkingEvent', (_, payload) => {
  window.dispatchEvent(new CustomEvent('gangstalkingEvent', { detail: payload }));
});

settingsAPI.js
js


Copy
const fs = require('fs');
const path = require('path');

function getSettingsPath(profile) {
  return path.join(__dirname, 'data', 'profiles', profile, 'settings.json');
}

function ensureProfileDir(profile) {
  const dir = path.join(__dirname, 'data', 'profiles', profile);
  if (!fs.existsSync(dir)) {
    fs.mkdirSync(dir, { recursive: true });
  }
}

async function loadSettings(profile) {
  ensureProfileDir(profile);
  const p = getSettingsPath(profile);

  if (!fs.existsSync(p)) {
    const defaults = {
      theme: "theme.default",
      overlayEnabled: true,
      grokBuddyEnabled: true,
      redMode: false,
      gangstalkingMode: true,
      pluginsEnabled: {},
      panicMeterEnabled: true
    };

    fs.writeFileSync(p, JSON.stringify(defaults, null, 2));
    return defaults;
  }

  return JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(p, 'utf8'));
}

async function saveSettings(profile, settings) {
  ensureProfileDir(profile);
  const p = getSettingsPath(profile);
  fs.writeFileSync(p, JSON.stringify(settings, null, 2), 'utf8');
}

module.exports = {
  loadSettings,
  saveSettings
};

profileAPI.js
js


Copy
const fs = require('fs');
const path = require('path');

const profilesRoot = path.join(__dirname, 'data', 'profiles');
const activeProfilePath = path.join(__dirname, 'data', 'activeProfile.json');

// Ensure /data/profiles exists
function ensureProfilesRoot() {
  if (!fs.existsSync(profilesRoot)) {
    fs.mkdirSync(profilesRoot, { recursive: true });
  }
}

// Ensure a specific profile folder exists
function ensureProfileDir(profile) {
  const dir = path.join(profilesRoot, profile);
  if (!fs.existsSync(dir)) {
    fs.mkdirSync(dir, { recursive: true });
  }
  return dir;
}

// Load the currently active profile
function loadActiveProfile() {
  ensureProfilesRoot();

  if (!fs.existsSync(activeProfilePath)) {
    // Default profile if none exists
    const defaultProfile = { active: "default" };
    fs.writeFileSync(activeProfilePath, JSON.stringify(defaultProfile, null, 2));
    ensureProfileDir("default");
    return "default";
  }

  const data = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(activeProfilePath, 'utf8'));
  ensureProfileDir(data.active);
  return data.active;
}

// Save the active profile
function saveActiveProfile(profile) {
  ensureProfilesRoot();
  ensureProfileDir(profile);

  const data = { active: profile };
  fs.writeFileSync(activeProfilePath, JSON.stringify(data, null, 2));
}

// List all profiles
function listProfiles() {
  ensureProfilesRoot();
  return fs.readdirSync(profilesRoot)
    .filter(name => fs.lstatSync(path.join(profilesRoot, name)).isDirectory());
}

// Switch to a different profile
function switchProfile(profile) {
  saveActiveProfile(profile);
}

module.exports = {
  loadActiveProfile,
  saveActiveProfile,
  listProfiles,
  switchProfile,
  ensureProfileDir
};

📄 trackerService.js
This file powers the Gangstalking Dashboard.

goonSpike

trackerService.js
js


Copy
const fs = require('fs');
const path = require('path');
const { eventBus } = require('./eventBus');
const { loadActiveProfile } = require('./profileAPI');
const { loadSettings } = require('./settingsAPI');
const { batchPoll } = require('./utils/pollingBatcher');

function getTrackedPeoplePath(profile) {
  return path.join(__dirname, 'data', 'profiles', profile, 'trackedPeople.json');
}

function ensureTrackedPeople(profile) {
  const p = getTrackedPeoplePath(profile);
  if (!fs.existsSync(p)) {
    fs.writeFileSync(p, JSON.stringify([], null, 2));
  }
}

async function loadTrackedPeople() {
  const profile = await loadActiveProfile();
  ensureTrackedPeople(profile);
  const p = getTrackedPeoplePath(profile);
  return JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(p, 'utf8'));
}

async function saveTrackedPeople(list) {
  const profile = await loadActiveProfile();
  const p = getTrackedPeoplePath(profile);
  fs.writeFileSync(p, JSON.stringify(list, null, 2));
}

//
// POLLING ENGINE
//

let pollingInterval = null;

async function startPolling() {
  const profile = await loadActiveProfile();
  const settings = await loadSettings(profile);
  const tracked = await loadTrackedPeople();

  if (!tracked.length) return;

  // Red Mode threshold adjustments
  const dramaThreshold = settings.redMode ? 2 : 5;
  const goonThreshold = settings.redMode ? 4 : 10;
  const meltdownThreshold = settings.redMode ? 3 : 7;

  pollingInterval = setInterval(async () => {
    const results = await batchPoll(tracked);

    results.forEach(result => {
      const { personId, newItems } = result;

      if (newItems.length > 0) {
        eventBus.publish('newActivity', { personId, items: newItems });
      }

      // Goon spike detection
      if (newItems.length >= goonThreshold) {
        eventBus.publish('goonSpike', { personId, count: newItems.length });
      }

      // Lolcow spike detection
      if (newItems.length >= goonThreshold * 2) {
        eventBus.publish('lolcowSpike', { personId, count: newItems.length });
      }

      // Drama spike detection
      const dramaScore = newItems.filter(i => i.type === 'post').length;
      if (dramaScore >= dramaThreshold) {
        eventBus.publish('dramaSpike', { personId, score: dramaScore });
      }

      // Meltdown detection
      if (dramaScore >= meltdownThreshold) {
        eventBus.publish('meltdownDetected', { personId });
      }
    });

  }, 5000);
}

function stopPolling() {
  if (pollingInterval) clearInterval(pollingInterval);
}

module.exports = {
  loadTrackedPeople,
  saveTrackedPeople,
  startPolling,
  stopPolling
};

analyticsService.js
js


Copy
const fs = require('fs');
const path = require('path');
const { eventBus } = require('./eventBus');
const { loadActiveProfile } = require('./profileAPI');
const { loadSettings } = require('./settingsAPI');

function getAnalyticsPath(profile) {
  return path.join(__dirname, 'data', 'profiles', profile, 'analytics.json');
}

function ensureAnalytics(profile) {
  const p = getAnalyticsPath(profile);
  if (!fs.existsSync(p)) {
    fs.writeFileSync(p, JSON.stringify({
      history: [],
      spikes: [],
      meltdowns: []
    }, null, 2));
  }
}

async function loadAnalytics() {
  const profile = await loadActiveProfile();
  ensureAnalytics(profile);
  const p = getAnalyticsPath(profile);
  return JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(p, 'utf8'));
}

async function saveAnalytics(data) {
  const profile = await loadActiveProfile();
  const p = getAnalyticsPath(profile);
  fs.writeFileSync(p, JSON.stringify(data, null, 2));
}

//
// ANALYTICS ENGINE
//

async function initAnalyticsEngine() {
  const profile = await loadActiveProfile();
  const settings = await loadSettings(profile);

  const analytics = await loadAnalytics();

  const dramaThreshold = settings.redMode ? 2 : 5;
  const goonThreshold = settings.redMode ? 4 : 10;
  const meltdownThreshold = settings.redMode ? 3 : 7;

  //
  // NEW ACTIVITY
  //
  eventBus.subscribe('newActivity', async ({ personId, items }) => {
    analytics.history.push({
      timestamp: Date.now(),
      personId,
      count: items.length
    });

    await saveAnalytics(analytics);
  });

  //
  // GOON SPIKE
  //
  eventBus.subscribe('goonSpike', async ({ personId, count }) => {
    analytics.spikes.push({
      type: "goon",
      timestamp: Date.now(),
      personId,
      count
    });

    await saveAnalytics(analytics);
  });

  //
  // LOLCOW SPIKE
  //
  eventBus.subscribe('lolcowSpike', async ({ personId, count }) => {
    analytics.spikes.push({
      type: "lolcow",
      timestamp: Date.now(),
      personId,
      count
    });

    await saveAnalytics(analytics);
  });

  //
  // DRAMA SPIKE
  //
  eventBus.subscribe('dramaSpike', async ({ personId, score }) => {
    analytics.spikes.push({
      type: "drama",
      timestamp: Date.now(),
      personId,
      score
    });

    await saveAnalytics(analytics);
  });

  //
  // MELTDOWN DETECTED
  //
  eventBus.subscribe('meltdownDetected', async ({ personId }) => {
    analytics.meltdowns.push({
      timestamp: Date.now(),
      personId
    });

    await saveAnalytics(analytics);
  });
}

module.exports = {
  initAnalyticsEngine,
  loadAnalytics,
  saveAnalytics
};

pluginLoader.js
js


Copy
const fs = require('fs');
const path = require('path');
const { loadActiveProfile } = require('./profileAPI');
const { loadSettings } = require('./settingsAPI');

function getPluginsRoot() {
  return path.join(__dirname, 'plugins');
}

function loadPluginManifest(pluginDir) {
  const manifestPath = path.join(pluginDir, 'plugin.json');
  if (!fs.existsSync(manifestPath)) return null;
  return JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(manifestPath, 'utf8'));
}

function loadPluginMain(pluginDir) {
  const mainPath = path.join(pluginDir, 'main.js');
  if (!fs.existsSync(mainPath)) return null;
  return require(mainPath);
}

async function initPluginLoader(profile, settings, eventBus) {
  const pluginsRoot = getPluginsRoot();
  const pluginDirs = fs.readdirSync(pluginsRoot)
    .map(name => path.join(pluginsRoot, name))
    .filter(dir => fs.lstatSync(dir).isDirectory());

  for (const dir of pluginDirs) {
    const manifest = loadPluginManifest(dir);
    if (!manifest) continue;

    // Check if plugin is enabled for this profile
    const enabled = settings.pluginsEnabled?.[manifest.id] ?? true;
    if (!enabled) continue;

    const pluginMain = loadPluginMain(dir);
    if (!pluginMain) continue;

    try {
      pluginMain({
        eventBus,
        profile,
        settings,
        manifest,
        pluginDir: dir
      });

      console.log(`Loaded plugin: ${manifest.name}`);
    } catch (err) {
      console.error(`Plugin failed to load: ${manifest?.name}`, err);
    }
  }
}

module.exports = {
  initPluginLoader
};

//
// INITIALIZATION
//

const contentFrame = document.getElementById("content-frame");
const themeCss = document.getElementById("theme-css");

async function init() {
  const settings = await appAPI.loadSettings();
  loadTheme(settings.theme);

  // Red Mode initial state
  if (settings.redMode) {
    document.body.classList.add("redmode");
  }

  setupNavigation();
  setupButtons();
}

init();


//
// THEME LOADING
//

function loadTheme(themeId) {
  const themePath = `../themes/${themeId.split('.')[1]}/theme.css`;
  themeCss.href = themePath;
}


//
// NAVIGATION
//

function setupNavigation() {
  const navButtons = document.querySelectorAll(".nav-btn");

  navButtons.forEach(btn => {
    btn.addEventListener("click", () => {
      const target = btn.dataset.target;

      switch (target) {
        case "dashboard":
          contentFrame.src = "windows/gangstalkingDashboard.html";
          break;

        case "tracked":
          contentFrame.src = "windows/trackedPeople.html";
          break;

        case "plugins":
          contentFrame.src = "windows/plugins.html";
          break;

        case "themes":
          contentFrame.src = "windows/themes.html";
          break;
      }
    });
  });
}


//
// BUTTONS
//

function setupButtons() {
  document.getElementById("btn-settings").addEventListener("click", () => {
    contentFrame.src = "windows/settings.html";
  });

  document.getElementById("btn-profiles").addEventListener("click", () => {
    contentFrame.src = "windows/profileManager.html";
  });

  document.getElementById("btn-analytics").addEventListener("click", () => {
    contentFrame.src = "windows/analytics.html";
  });

  document.getElementById("btn-grok").addEventListener("click", () => {
    appAPI.sendIPC("openGrokBuddy");
  });

  document.getElementById("btn-redmode").addEventListener("click", async () => {
    const settings = await appAPI.loadSettings();
    settings.redMode = !settings.redMode;
    await appAPI.saveSettings(settings);

    appAPI.onEvent("redModeToggled", { enabled: settings.redMode });

    if (settings.redMode) {
      document.body.classList.add("redmode");
    } else {
      document.body.classList.remove("redmode");
    }
  });
}


//
// RED MODE EVENT HANDLING
//

window.addEventListener("redModeToggled", (e) => {
  const enabled = e.detail.enabled;

  if (enabled) {
    document.body.classList.add("redmode");
  } else {
    document.body.classList.remove("redmode");
  }
});

Copy
//
// ELEMENTS
//

const trackedContainer = document.getElementById("tracked-container");
const activityContainer = document.getElementById("activity-container");
const addPersonBtn = document.getElementById("btn-add-person");


//
// LOAD TRACKED PEOPLE
//

async function loadTrackedPeople() {
  const people = await appAPI.loadTrackedPeople();
  renderTrackedPeople(people);
}

function renderTrackedPeople(list) {
  trackedContainer.innerHTML = "";

  list.forEach(person => {
    const div = document.createElement("div");
    div.className = "tracked-person";

    div.innerHTML = `
      <div class="name">${person.displayName}</div>
      <div class="id">${person.id}</div>
      <button class="remove-btn" data-id="${person.id}">Remove</button>
    `;

    trackedContainer.appendChild(div);
  });

  // Remove handlers
  document.querySelectorAll(".remove-btn").forEach(btn => {
    btn.addEventListener("click", async () => {
      const id = btn.dataset.id;
      const people = await appAPI.loadTrackedPeople();
      const updated = people.filter(p => p.id !== id);
      await appAPI.saveTrackedPeople(updated);
      loadTrackedPeople();
    });
  });
}


//
// ACTIVITY FEED
//

function addActivityItem(personId, items) {
  const div = document.createElement("div");
  div.className = "activity-item";

  const count = items.length;
  const time = new Date().toLocaleTimeString();

  div.innerHTML = `
    <div class="activity-header">
      <span class="person">${personId}</span>
      <span class="time">${time}</span>
    </div>
    <div class="activity-body">${count} new items</div>
  `;

  activityContainer.prepend(div);
}


//
// EVENT HANDLERS
//

// New activity
appAPI.onEvent("newActivity", ({ personId, items }) => {
  addActivityItem(personId, items);
});

// Goon spike
appAPI.onEvent("goonSpike", ({ personId, count }) => {
  addActivityItem(personId, [{}, {}, {}]); // visual bump
  flashAlert(`GOON SPIKE: ${personId} (${count})`);
});

// Lolcow spike
appAPI.onEvent("lolcowSpike", ({ personId, count }) => {
  addActivityItem(personId, [{}, {}, {}, {}, {}]);
  flashAlert(`LOLCOW SPIKE: ${personId} (${count})`);
});

// Drama spike
appAPI.onEvent("dramaSpike", ({ personId, score }) => {
  flashAlert(`DRAMA SPIKE: ${personId} (${score})`);
});

// Meltdown detected
appAPI.onEvent("meltdownDetected", ({ personId }) => {
  flashAlert(`MELTDOWN DETECTED: ${personId}`);
});


//
// RED MODE VISUALS
//

window.addEventListener("redModeToggled", (e) => {
  const enabled = e.detail.enabled;
  if (enabled) {
    document.body.classList.add("redmode");
  } else {
    document.body.classList.remove("redmode");
  }
});


//
// ADD PERSON
//

addPersonBtn.addEventListener("click", async () => {
  const name = prompt("Enter display name:");
  const id = prompt("Enter ID/handle:");

  if (!name || !id) return;

  const people = await appAPI.loadTrackedPeople();
  people.push({ displayName: name, id });
  await appAPI.saveTrackedPeople(people);

  loadTrackedPeople();
});


//
// ALERT FLASH
//

function flashAlert(text) {
  const div = document.createElement("div");
  div.className = "alert-flash";
  div.textContent = text;

  document.body.appendChild(div);

  setTimeout(() => div.remove(), 3000);
}


//
// INIT
//

loadTrackedPeople();

📄 renderer/windows/analytics.js
This file powers the Gangstalking Insights window.
It handles:

Loading analytics data

Rendering:

Activity history

Spike logs

Meltdown logs

Reacting to Red Mode

Updating the UI live when analytics events fire

Providing a clean, readable insights panel

This is the logic layer for the analytics window.

renderer/windows/analytics.js
js


Copy
//
// ELEMENTS
//

const historyList = document.getElementById("history-list");
const spikeList = document.getElementById("spike-list");
const meltdownList = document.getElementById("meltdown-list");


//
// LOAD ANALYTICS
//

async function loadAnalytics() {
  const analytics = await appAPI.loadAnalytics();
  renderHistory(analytics.history);
  renderSpikes(analytics.spikes);
  renderMeltdowns(analytics.meltdowns);
}

//
// RENDER FUNCTIONS
//

function renderHistory(history) {
  historyList.innerHTML = "";

  history
    .slice()
    .reverse()
    .forEach(entry => {
      const div = document.createElement("div");
      div.className = "history-item";

      const time = new Date(entry.timestamp).toLocaleString();

      div.innerHTML = `
        <div class="row">
          <span class="label">Person:</span>
          <span class="value">${entry.personId}</span>
        </div>
        <div class="row">
          <span class="label">Items:</span>
          <span class="value">${entry.count}</span>
        </div>
        <div class="row">
          <span class="label">Time:</span>
          <span class="value">${time}</span>
        </div>
      `;

      historyList.appendChild(div);
    });
}

function renderSpikes(spikes) {
  spikeList.innerHTML = "";

  spikes
    .slice()
    .reverse()
    .forEach(spike => {
      const div = document.createElement("div");
      div.className = `spike-item spike-${spike.type}`;

      const time = new Date(spike.timestamp).toLocaleString();

      div.innerHTML = `
        <div class="row">
          <span class="label">Type:</span>
          <span class="value">${spike.type.toUpperCase()}</span>
        </div>
        <div class="row">
          <span class="label">Person:</span>
          <span class="value">${spike.personId}</span>
        </div>
        <div class="row">
          <span class="label">Value:</span>
          <span class="value">${spike.count || spike.score}</span>
        </div>
        <div class="row">
          <span class="label">Time:</span>
          <span class="value">${time}</span>
        </div>
      `;

      spikeList.appendChild(div);
    });
}

function renderMeltdowns(meltdowns) {
  meltdownList.innerHTML = "";

  meltdowns
    .slice()
    .reverse()
    .forEach(m => {
      const div = document.createElement("div");
      div.className = "meltdown-item";

      const time = new Date(m.timestamp).toLocaleString();

      div.innerHTML = `
        <div class="row">
          <span class="label">Person:</span>
          <span class="value">${m.personId}</span>
        </div>
        <div class="row">
          <span class="label">Time:</span>
          <span class="value">${time}</span>
        </div>
      `;

      meltdownList.appendChild(div);
    });
}


//
// LIVE EVENT UPDATES
//

appAPI.onEvent("newActivity", async () => {
  const analytics = await appAPI.loadAnalytics();
  renderHistory(analytics.history);
});

appAPI.onEvent("goonSpike", async () => {
  const analytics = await appAPI.loadAnalytics();
  renderSpikes(analytics.spikes);
});

appAPI.onEvent("lolcowSpike", async () => {
  const analytics = await appAPI.loadAnalytics();
  renderSpikes(analytics.spikes);
});

appAPI.onEvent("dramaSpike", async () => {
  const analytics = await appAPI.loadAnalytics();
  renderSpikes(analytics.spikes);
});

appAPI.onEvent("meltdownDetected", async () => {
  const analytics = await appAPI.loadAnalytics();
  renderMeltdowns(analytics.meltdowns);
});


//
// RED MODE VISUALS
//

window.addEventListener("redModeToggled", (e) => {
  const enabled = e.detail.enabled;
  if (enabled) {
    document.body.classList.add("redmode");
  } else {
    document.body.classList.remove("redmode");
  }
});


//
// INIT
//

loadAnalytics();

📄 renderer/windows/settings.js
This file powers the Settings Window.
It handles:

Loading settings

Populating the UI

Loading available themes

Saving settings

Triggering Red Mode events

Updating the renderer theme

Syncing with the profile system

This is the logic layer for the settings panel.

renderer/windows/settings.js
js


Copy
//
// ELEMENTS
//

const themeSelect = document.getElementById("theme-select");
const toggleRedMode = document.getElementById("toggle-redmode");
const toggleGS = document.getElementById("toggle-gs");
const toggleOverlay = document.getElementById("toggle-overlay");
const toggleGrok = document.getElementById("toggle-grok");
const togglePanic = document.getElementById("toggle-panic");
const saveBtn = document.getElementById("btn-save");


//
// LOAD SETTINGS
//

async function loadSettingsUI() {
  const settings = await appAPI.loadSettings();

  // Theme
  await loadThemes(settings.theme);

  // Toggles
  toggleRedMode.checked = settings.redMode;
  toggleGS.checked = settings.gangstalkingMode;
  toggleOverlay.checked = settings.overlayEnabled;
  toggleGrok.checked = settings.grokBuddyEnabled;
  togglePanic.checked = settings.panicMeterEnabled;
}

loadSettingsUI();


//
// LOAD THEMES
//

async function loadThemes(activeTheme) {
  // Hardcoded theme list for now
  const themes = [
    { id: "theme.default", name: "Default" },
    { id: "theme.dark", name: "Dark" },
    { id: "theme.red", name: "Red Mode" }
  ];

  themeSelect.innerHTML = "";

  themes.forEach(t => {
    const opt = document.createElement("option");
    opt.value = t.id;
    opt.textContent = t.name;
    if (t.id === activeTheme) opt.selected = true;
    themeSelect.appendChild(opt);
  });
}


//
// SAVE SETTINGS
//

saveBtn.addEventListener("click", async () => {
  const settings = await appAPI.loadSettings();

  settings.theme = themeSelect.value;
  settings.redMode = toggleRedMode.checked;
  settings.gangstalkingMode = toggleGS.checked;
  settings.overlayEnabled = toggleOverlay.checked;
  settings.grokBuddyEnabled = toggleGrok.checked;
  settings.panicMeterEnabled = togglePanic.checked;

  await appAPI.saveSettings(settings);

  // Notify Red Mode listeners
  appAPI.sendIPC("redModeToggled", { enabled: settings.redMode });

  alert("Settings saved.");
});
✔ What this file enables
🔧 Settings Management

🎨 Theme System

🔥 Red Mode
Toggles Red Mode

Updates renderer windows

🛰 Gangstalking Mode
Enables/disables the entire subsystem

Toggles Grok Buddy availability

📊 Overlay + Panic Meter
Toggles overlay HUD

Toggles panic meter

This file is the control panel logic for the entire app.

📄 renderer/windows/profileManager.js
This file powers the Profile Manager window.
It handles:

Listing all profiles

Highlighting the active profile

Switching profiles

Creating new profiles

Deleting profiles

Triggering a full app reload on profile switch

Syncing with profileAPI + settingsAPI

This is the logic layer for the multi‑profile system.

renderer/windows/profileManager.js
js


Copy
//
// ELEMENTS
//

const profileList = document.getElementById("profile-list");
const newProfileBtn = document.getElementById("btn-new-profile");


//
// LOAD PROFILES
//

async function loadProfiles() {
  const active = await appAPI.loadActiveProfile();
  const profiles = await appAPI.listProfiles();

  profileList.innerHTML = "";

  profiles.forEach(name => {
    const div = document.createElement("div");
    div.className = "profile-item";

    if (name === active) {
      div.classList.add("active");
    }

    div.innerHTML = `
      <div class="profile-name">${name}</div>
      <div class="profile-actions">
        <button class="switch-btn" data-name="${name}">Switch</button>
        <button class="delete-btn" data-name="${name}">Delete</button>
      </div>
    `;

    profileList.appendChild(div);
  });

  setupActionHandlers();
}

loadProfiles();


//
// ACTION HANDLERS
//

function setupActionHandlers() {
  // Switch profile
  document.querySelectorAll(".switch-btn").forEach(btn => {
    btn.addEventListener("click", async () => {
      const name = btn.dataset.name;
      await appAPI.switchProfile(name);

      // Reload entire app
      location.reload();
    });
  });

  // Delete profile
  document.querySelectorAll(".delete-btn").forEach(btn => {
    btn.addEventListener("click", async () => {
      const name = btn.dataset.name;

      if (!confirm(`Delete profile "${name}"?`)) return;

      const profiles = await appAPI.listProfiles();
      const remaining = profiles.filter(p => p !== name);

      // Delete folder
      await appAPI.sendIPC("deleteProfile", { name });

      // If active profile was deleted, switch to first remaining
      const active = await appAPI.loadActiveProfile();
      if (active === name && remaining.length > 0) {
        await appAPI.switchProfile(remaining[0]);
      }

      location.reload();
    });
  });
}


//
// CREATE NEW PROFILE
//

newProfileBtn.addEventListener("click", async () => {
  const name = prompt("Enter new profile name:");
  if (!name) return;

  const profiles = await appAPI.listProfiles();
  if (profiles.includes(name)) {
    alert("Profile already exists.");
    return;
  }

  // Create by switching to it (auto‑creates folder)
  await appAPI.switchProfile(name);

  location.reload();
});

Switching profiles triggers:

New settings

🔥 Integration

This file is the control center for profile management.

📄 renderer/windows/trackedPeople.js
This file powers the Tracked People management window.
It handles:

renderer/windows/trackedPeople.js
js


Copy
//
// ELEMENTS
//

const trackedContainer = document.getElementById("tracked-container");
const addBtn = document.getElementById("btn-add");


//
// LOAD TRACKED PEOPLE
//

async function loadTrackedPeople() {
  const people = await appAPI.loadTrackedPeople();
  renderPeople(people);
}

loadTrackedPeople();


//
// RENDER
//

function renderPeople(list) {
  trackedContainer.innerHTML = "";

  list.forEach(person => {
    const div = document.createElement("div");
    div.className = "tracked-item";

    div.innerHTML = `
      <div class="info">
        <div class="name">${person.displayName}</div>
        <div class="id">${person.id}</div>
      </div>
      <button class="remove-btn" data-id="${person.id}">Remove</button>
    `;

    trackedContainer.appendChild(div);
  });

  setupRemoveHandlers();
}


//
// REMOVE PERSON
//

function setupRemoveHandlers() {
  document.querySelectorAll(".remove-btn").forEach(btn => {
    btn.addEventListener("click", async () => {
      const id = btn.dataset.id;

      const people = await appAPI.loadTrackedPeople();
      const updated = people.filter(p => p.id !== id);

      await appAPI.saveTrackedPeople(updated);
      loadTrackedPeople();
    });
  });
}


//
// ADD PERSON
//

addBtn.addEventListener("click", async () => {
  const name = prompt("Enter display name:");
  const id = prompt("Enter ID/handle:");

  if (!name || !id) return;

  const people = await appAPI.loadTrackedPeople();
  people.push({ displayName: name, id });

  await appAPI.saveTrackedPeople(people);
  loadTrackedPeople();
});


//
// RED MODE VISUALS
//

window.addEventListener("redModeToggled", (e) => {
  const enabled = e.detail.enabled;
  if (enabled) {
    document.body.classList.add("redmode");
  } else {
    document.body.classList.remove("redmode");
  }
});

📄 renderer/windows/plugins.js
This file powers the Plugin Manager window.
It handles:

renderer/windows/plugins.js
js


Copy
//
// ELEMENTS
//

const pluginList = document.getElementById("plugin-list");


//
// LOAD PLUGINS
//

async function loadPlugins() {
  const settings = await appAPI.loadSettings();
  const enabled = settings.enabledPlugins || [];

  const plugins = await appAPI.listPlugins(); 
  // returns array of:
  // { id, name, version, description }

  renderPlugins(plugins, enabled);
}

loadPlugins();


//
// RENDER
//

function renderPlugins(plugins, enabledList) {
  pluginList.innerHTML = "";

  plugins.forEach(plugin => {
    const div = document.createElement("div");
    div.className = "plugin-item";

    const isEnabled = enabledList.includes(plugin.id);

    div.innerHTML = `
      <div class="info">
        <div class="name">${plugin.name}</div>
        <div class="meta">
          <span class="version">v${plugin.version}</span>
        </div>
        <div class="desc">${plugin.description}</div>
      </div>

      <label class="toggle">
        <input type="checkbox" class="plugin-toggle" data-id="${plugin.id}" ${isEnabled ? "checked" : ""} />
        <span>Enabled</span>
      </label>
    `;

    pluginList.appendChild(div);
  });

  setupToggleHandlers();
}


//
// ENABLE / DISABLE PLUGINS
//

function setupToggleHandlers() {
  document.querySelectorAll(".plugin-toggle").forEach(toggle => {
    toggle.addEventListener("change", async () => {
      const id = toggle.dataset.id;
      const settings = await appAPI.loadSettings();

      if (!settings.enabledPlugins) {
        settings.enabledPlugins = [];
      }

      if (toggle.checked) {
        if (!settings.enabledPlugins.includes(id)) {
          settings.enabledPlugins.push(id);
        }
      } else {
        settings.enabledPlugins = settings.enabledPlugins.filter(p => p !== id);
      }

      await appAPI.saveSettings(settings);

      // Reload plugins in main process
      appAPI.sendIPC("reloadPlugins");
    });
  });
}


//
// RED MODE VISUALS
//

window.addEventListener("redModeToggled", (e) => {
  const enabled = e.detail.enabled;
  if (enabled) {
    document.body.classList.add("redmode");
  } else {
    document.body.classList.remove("redmode");
  }
});

📄 renderer/windows/overlay.js
This is the logic engine for the Overlay HUD.
It handles:

Panic Meter updates

Spike alerts

Grok Buddy reactions

Red Mode visual changes
