renderer/windows/overlay.js
js


Copy
//
// ELEMENTS
//

const panicMeter = document.getElementById("panic-meter");
const panicBar = document.getElementById("panic-bar");
const spikeAlerts = document.getElementById("spike-alerts");
const grokReaction = document.getElementById("grok-reaction");


//
// SETTINGS SYNC
//

async function applySettings() {
  const settings = await appAPI.loadSettings();

  // Panic Meter
  if (settings.panicMeterEnabled) {
    panicMeter.classList.remove("hidden");
  } else {
    panicMeter.classList.add("hidden");
  }

  // Grok Buddy reactions
  if (!settings.grokBuddyEnabled) {
    grokReaction.classList.add("hidden");
  }
}

applySettings();


//
// PANIC METER
//

appAPI.onEvent("panicLevelChanged", ({ level }) => {
  const pct = Math.min(100, Math.max(0, level));
  panicBar.style.width = pct + "%";

  if (pct > 80) {
    panicMeter.classList.add("danger");
  } else {
    panicMeter.classList.remove("danger");
  }
});


//
// SPIKE ALERTS
//

function showSpikeAlert(text) {
  const div = document.createElement("div");
  div.className = "spike-alert";
  div.textContent = text;

  spikeAlerts.appendChild(div);

  setTimeout(() => {
    div.classList.add("fade");
    setTimeout(() => div.remove(), 500);
  }, 2000);
}

appAPI.onEvent("goonSpike", ({ personId, count }) => {
  showSpikeAlert(`GOON SPIKE: ${personId} (${count})`);
});

appAPI.onEvent("lolcowSpike", ({ personId, count }) => {
  showSpikeAlert(`LOLCOW SPIKE: ${personId} (${count})`);
});

appAPI.onEvent("dramaSpike", ({ personId, score }) => {
  showSpikeAlert(`DRAMA SPIKE: ${personId} (${score})`);
});

appAPI.onEvent("meltdownDetected", ({ personId }) => {
  showSpikeAlert(`MELTDOWN: ${personId}`);
});


//
// GROK BUDDY REACTIONS
//

appAPI.onEvent("grokReaction", ({ text }) => {
  grokReaction.textContent = text;
  grokReaction.classList.remove("hidden");
  grokReaction.classList.add("visible");

  setTimeout(() => {
    grokReaction.classList.remove("visible");
    grokReaction.classList.add("hidden");
  }, 3000);
});


//
// RED MODE
//

window.addEventListener("redModeToggled", (e) => {
  const enabled = e.detail.enabled;
  if (enabled) {
    document.body.classList.add("redmode");
  } else {
    document.body.classList.remove("redmode");
  }
});

📄 renderer/windows/grokBuddy.js
js


Copy
//
// ELEMENTS
//

const avatar = document.getElementById("grok-avatar");
const textBox = document.getElementById("grok-textbox");
const textEl = document.getElementById("grok-text");


//
// STATE
//

let mood = "neutral"; 
let wisdom = 0;


//
// SETTINGS SYNC
//

async function applySettings() {
  const settings = await appAPI.loadSettings();

  if (!settings.grokBuddyEnabled) {
    document.body.classList.add("hidden");
  } else {
    document.body.classList.remove("hidden");
  }
}

applySettings();


//
// REACTION ENGINE
//

appAPI.onEvent("grokSay", ({ text, mood: newMood }) => {
  mood = newMood || "neutral";
  textEl.textContent = text;

  avatar.className = "mood-" + mood;

  textBox.classList.add("visible");
  setTimeout(() => textBox.classList.remove("visible"), 3000);
});


//
// WISDOM METER
//

appAPI.onEvent("grokWisdom", ({ amount }) => {
  wisdom += amount;
  if (wisdom > 100) wisdom = 100;
  if (wisdom < 0) wisdom = 0;

  avatar.style.filter = `hue-rotate(${wisdom * 3.6}deg)`;
});


//
// RED MODE
//

window.addEventListener("redModeToggled", (e) => {
  const enabled = e.detail.enabled;
  if (enabled) {
    document.body.classList.add("redmode");
  } else {
    document.body.classList.remove("redmode");
  }
});

📄 services/trackerService.js
js


Copy
const fs = require("fs");
const path = require("path");

class TrackerService {
  constructor(profilePath) {
    this.file = path.join(profilePath, "tracked.json");
    if (!fs.existsSync(this.file)) {
      fs.writeFileSync(this.file, "[]");
    }
  }

  load() {
    return JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(this.file, "utf8"));
  }

  save(list) {
    fs.writeFileSync(this.file, JSON.stringify(list, null, 2));
  }

  add(person) {
    const list = this.load();
    list.push(person);
    this.save(list);
  }

  remove(id) {
    const list = this.load().filter(p => p.id !== id);
    this.save(list);
  }
}

module.exports = TrackerService;
📄 services/settingsService.js
js


Copy
const fs = require("fs");
const path = require("path");

class SettingsService {
  constructor(profilePath) {
    this.file = path.join(profilePath, "settings.json");
    if (!fs.existsSync(this.file)) {
      fs.writeFileSync(this.file, JSON.stringify({
        theme: "theme.default",
        redMode: false,
        gangstalkingMode: false,
        overlayEnabled: true,
        grokBuddyEnabled: true,
        panicMeterEnabled: true,
        enabledPlugins: []
      }, null, 2));
    }
  }

  load() {
    return JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(this.file, "utf8"));
  }

  save(settings) {
    fs.writeFileSync(this.file, JSON.stringify(settings, null, 2));
  }
}

module.exports = SettingsService;
📄 services/profileService.js
js


Copy
const fs = require("fs");
const path = require("path");

class ProfileService {
  constructor(root) {
    this.root = root;
    this.activeFile = path.join(root, "activeProfile.txt");

    if (!fs.existsSync(this.activeFile)) {
      fs.writeFileSync(this.activeFile, "default");
    }
  }

  list() {
    return fs.readdirSync(this.root).filter(f =>
      fs.statSync(path.join(this.root, f)).isDirectory()
    );
  }

  active() {
    return fs.readFileSync(this.activeFile, "utf8").trim();
  }

  switch(name) {
    fs.writeFileSync(this.activeFile, name);
  }
}

module.exports = ProfileService;
📄 pluginLoader.js
js


Copy
const fs = require("fs");
const path = require("path");

class PluginLoader {
  constructor(dir) {
    this.dir = dir;
  }

  list() {
    if (!fs.existsSync(this.dir)) return [];
    return fs.readdirSync(this.dir)
      .filter(f => f.endsWith(".js"))
      .map(f => {
        const mod = require(path.join(this.dir, f));
        return {
          id: mod.id,
          name: mod.name,
          version: mod.version,
          description: mod.description
        };
      });
  }

  loadEnabled(enabledList) {
    enabledList.forEach(id => {
      const file = path.join(this.dir, id + ".js");
      if (fs.existsSync(file)) {
        require(file).init();
      }
    });
  }
}

module.exports = PluginLoader;
📄 main.js
js


Copy
const { app, BrowserWindow, ipcMain } = require("electron");
const path = require("path");

const ProfileService = require("./services/profileService");
const SettingsService = require("./services/settingsService");
const TrackerService = require("./services/trackerService");
const PluginLoader = require("./pluginLoader");

let mainWindow;
let overlayWindow;

const profiles = new ProfileService(path.join(__dirname, "profiles"));

function loadProfileServices() {
  const active = profiles.active();
  const profilePath = path.join(__dirname, "profiles", active);

  return {
    settings: new SettingsService(profilePath),
    tracker: new TrackerService(profilePath),
    plugins: new PluginLoader(path.join(profilePath, "plugins"))
  };
}

function createMainWindow() {
  mainWindow = new BrowserWindow({
    width: 1200,
    height: 800,
    webPreferences: {
      preload: path.join(__dirname, "preload.js")
    }
  });

  mainWindow.loadFile("renderer/windows/dashboard.html");
}

function createOverlayWindow() {
  overlayWindow = new BrowserWindow({
    width: 800,
    height: 600,
    frame: false,
    transparent: true,
    alwaysOnTop: true,
    webPreferences: {
      preload: path.join(__dirname, "preload.js")
    }
  });

  overlayWindow.loadFile("renderer/windows/overlay.html");
}

app.whenReady().then(() => {
  createMainWindow();
  createOverlayWindow();
});
📄 preload.js
js


Copy
const { contextBridge, ipcRenderer } = require("electron");

contextBridge.exposeInMainWorld("appAPI", {
  sendIPC: (channel, data) => ipcRenderer.send(channel, data),
  onEvent: (channel, fn) => ipcRenderer.on(channel, (_, data) => fn(data)),

  loadSettings: () => ipcRenderer.invoke("loadSettings"),
  saveSettings: (s) => ipcRenderer.invoke("saveSettings", s),

  loadTrackedPeople: () => ipcRenderer.invoke("loadTrackedPeople"),
  saveTrackedPeople: (p) => ipcRenderer.invoke("saveTrackedPeople", p),

  listPlugins: () => ipcRenderer.invoke("listPlugins"),

  loadActiveProfile: () => ipcRenderer.invoke("loadActiveProfile"),
  listProfiles: () => ipcRenderer.invoke("listProfiles"),
  switchProfile: (name) => ipcRenderer.invoke("switchProfile", name)
});
